Section P
September 1951 - July 1969
P-1 through P-____?

Public release photos of JPL projects, visitors to JPL, portraits and group photos of employees, social events, club activities, early facilities photos,  ...

There are 17 P-numbered photo albums ... when visiting the Archives to view photos, please request specific photo album numbers, such as photo album P1, or P17.

Dates seen in the index are the dates the photographs were entered into the Photo Lab index and filed.  This is not necessarily the date the photo was actually taken.

(U) - Unclassified
